【何尼玛】扭曲体;mso-font-kerning:1.0pt;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:华文中宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:华文中宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:0cm;text-align:left;
text-indent:0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:1;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1'><a
name="_Toc21544"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:黑体'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>一、<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><b><span
style='font-size:16.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>项目介绍</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc21544'></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc4258"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>1.1</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc4258'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>项目背景</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>坚持人与自然和谐共生。必须树立和<span class=GramE>践行</span>绿水青山就是金山银山的理念，坚持节约资源和保护环境的基本国策。基于此，国家领导人从国家高度对垃圾分类工作做出了重要指示，明确推行垃圾分类的重要性和必要性，中国垃圾分类进入了强制时代。截止到<span
lang=EN-US>2020</span>年<span lang=EN-US>6</span>月，虽然越来越多的城市开始实行垃圾分类政策，但如今垃圾分类的热度渐渐变小，人们对国家的垃圾分类相关政策也有些许不满。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc13663"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>1.2</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc13663'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>．项目介绍</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>本团队推出了小程序：垃圾分类<span class=GramE>趣</span>宝典，这是一款便于市民垃圾分类指南查询，并且培养用户垃圾分类意识为目的的小程序。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>其项目主要面向所处环境已强制实行垃圾分类政策的人群以及所处环境还未实行垃圾分类政策的人群，团队根据用户需求，制定了拍照、语音、文本方式的搜索功能，以便于使用者关于具体垃圾分类的查询，剧情测试功能让用户在娱乐的过程中可以了解一些科普知识，服务<span
class=GramE>集结站</span>提供用户关于垃圾分类的其他服务，每日一句关于保护环境的名言和图片培养用户垃圾分类意识以及漫画板块为用户持续更新有关为何要进行垃圾分类为主题的漫画。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc9369"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>1.3.</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc9369'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>项目意义</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>“垃圾分类<span class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”项目团队立志于让使用本小程序的用户，能多一点对国家垃圾分类政策的支持。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>虽然在如今垃圾分类政策初试行这个阶段，广大人民还看不见垃圾分类的最后成果，但是作为和国家跨出第一步的我们，应该与国家一起倡导垃圾分类政策，虽然如今国家的垃圾分类政策还未趋于完善，但这不应该成为广大人民不支持垃圾分类的原因，而应该成为人民支持垃圾分类，并且为垃圾分类做出自己的一份力量的原因，和国家一起进步。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>本项目团队希望让用户能逐渐意识到垃圾分类的重要性，以此为保护环境贡献自身的一份力量。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:0cm;text-align:left;
text-indent:0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:1;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1'><a
name="_Toc15048"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:黑体'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>二、<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><b><span
style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>需求分析</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc15048'></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:15.0pt;
font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc6167"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.1</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc6167'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>功能需求和非功能需求</span></b></span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.1.1</span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>功能需求<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>以下为“垃圾分类<span class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”的功能需求图：<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="图片_x0020_29" o:spid="_x0000_i1041" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:325.2pt;
 height:282.6pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="介绍文档.files/image003.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=434 height=377
src="介绍文档.files/image004.jpg" v:shapes="图片_x0020_29"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:
仿宋'>图<span lang=EN-US>2.1.1.</span>项目功能需求图<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.1.2.</span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>非功能需求<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>①观感需求<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>用户交互方式坚持以人性化的交互形式为主，配色以绿色为主打色，绿色是环保的颜色，传达清爽、希望、理想和生机勃勃的意象。<span
lang=EN-US>icon </span>以简约大方为主。四种垃圾分类的呈现方式将采取指南针的形式呈现。，象征保护环境是垃圾分类的指南针。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>②安全性需求<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>严格权限访问控制，用户在经过身份认证后，只能访问其权限范围内的数据，只能进行其权限范围内的操作。不同的用户具有不同的身份和权限，需要在用户身份真实可信的前提下，提供可信的授权管理服务，保护数据不被非法<span
lang=EN-US>/</span>越权访问和篡改，要确保数据的机密性和完整性。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>③可维护性需求<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>从接到修改请求后，对于普通修改应在<span lang=EN-US>1~2</span>天内完成；对于评估后为重大需求或设计修改应在<span
lang=EN-US>1</span>周内完成。<span lang=EN-US>90%</span>的<span lang=EN-US>BUG</span>修改时间不超过<span
lang=EN-US>1</span>个工作日，其他不超过<span lang=EN-US>2</span>个工作日。任何对象的任何方法都不允许超过<span
lang=EN-US>500</span>行代码。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc32328"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.2</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc32328'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>相似产品分析</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>目前，在线上平台中存在着许多提供垃圾分类指南查询的<span
lang=EN-US> app</span>、小程序。通过这些平台，用户能查询到自身想要查询的垃圾的具体分类。但大部分的<span lang=EN-US>
app </span>和小程序只注重用户“即用即走”的使用模式，没有注重其界面的美化和产品对其社会的意义所在。 <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
class=GramE><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:
【何尼玛】扭曲体'>微信小</span></span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;
mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>程序平台： <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>“垃圾分类指南”：简约界面，拥有强大的垃圾分类文本查询功能，中英文可切换，<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>有专题分类，垃圾分类测试等功能，界面相比于其他小程序来说较美化，功能相比于其他小程序来说，较全面。是一个提供“即用即走”使用模式的小程序中，做的较好的小程序。但缺少了拍照和语音识别的搜索功能，未加入更加多元化的搜索模式，不利于用户方便快捷的查询。
<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>App
</span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>平台：
<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>“垃圾分类”：在一加商店中，获垃圾分类专题中下载量最高<span
lang=EN-US> 3.2 </span>万次的<span lang=EN-US> App</span>。界面简单，也是一款单纯方便用户查询垃圾类别而量身定做的小程序。界面十分简洁，只有查询和测试两个功能。简洁化是其特点。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc30797"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.3</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc30797'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>使用人群</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.3.1.</span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>人群<span lang=EN-US>1</span>：有垃圾分类意识的人群<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>人群代表：小明、小红<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小明，<span
lang=EN-US>25</span>岁，工作场所在上海。一年前上海垃圾分类试运行，小明对垃圾分类进行了一些了解。了解了一些信息之后，了解到垃圾分类是为了缓解城市垃圾围城的现状，也有利于城市环境，故小<span
class=GramE>明对于</span>垃圾分类是相当的支持，也愿意来做这件事情。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=46 height=46
src="介绍文档.files/image008.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1039"><![endif]></span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小红：<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小红，<span
lang=EN-US>25</span>岁，工作场所在广州。一年前上海垃圾分类试运行，小红也因此对垃圾分类进行了一些了解，并且支持垃圾分类的这个政策。广州还没有开始进行强制垃圾分类，但是小红也已经在家中开始进行垃圾分类，并且收获了许多欢乐。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>对于小明、小红两位用户，小明和小红在面对垃圾桶进行垃圾分类时，忘记是什么类别时，可以进入“垃圾分类<span
class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”，利用<b>拍照识别</b>、<b>语音识别</b>或者是<b>文字形式</b>进行搜索，还可以在平日进入<b>“剧情”</b>的功能，在沉浸剧情的同时，得到一些关于垃圾分类的相关知识，并且可以在<b>“服务”</b>的功能寻找到垃圾分类的相关服务。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>2.3.2</span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>人群<span lang=EN-US>2</span>：未有垃圾分类意识的人群<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>人群代表：小花、小光<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span

src="介绍文档.files/image010.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1038"><![endif]></span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小花：<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小花，<span
lang=EN-US>30</span>岁。工作场所在广州。听闻上海垃圾分类强制实行，心想：“我们这么多年<span class=GramE>不</span>垃圾分类城市也好好的，为什么要垃圾分类，垃圾分类这么麻烦，我才不要进行垃圾分类呢。”<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

 <v:imagedata src="介绍文档.files/image011.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=47 height=47
src="介绍文档.files/image012.gif" alt=老男人 v:shapes="图片_x0020_31"><![endif]></span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小光：<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小光，<span
lang=EN-US>35</span>岁，在上海工作生活，上海垃圾分类强制实行之时，小光因新鲜感很热衷于垃圾分类，但当垃圾分类实行一段时间过后，小光听闻、也经历了垃圾分类许多不合理的地方，例如：源头垃圾分类，垃圾收运车运载时仍然将其堆放在一起运载，例如垃圾投放只能在规定的时间内进行投放，但其时间小光都要赶去上班，诸如此类的事情堆积起来小光对于垃圾分类<span
class=GramE>的怨念越来越</span>大。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>对于小花、小光这类的用户，在“垃圾分类<span
class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”中有开设<b>漫画</b>板块，为用户介绍垃圾分类的原因所在。以及“垃圾分类<span class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”中开设了“<b>每日一句</b>”的板块，倡导环保的意义，培养用户环境保护方面的社会责任感。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:0cm;text-align:left;
text-indent:0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:1;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1'><a
name="_Toc20387"><![if !supportLists]><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:仿宋'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>三、<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><![endif]><b><span
style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>产品介绍</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc20387'></span><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc22498"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>3.1</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc22498'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>功能介绍</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:28.0pt'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>下图为“垃圾分类<span
class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”的功能介绍：<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1036" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:436.2pt;height:366pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="介绍文档.files/image013.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=582 height=488
src="介绍文档.files/image014.jpg" v:shapes="_x0000_i1036"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:21.1pt;
mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><b><span style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:
仿宋'>图<span lang=EN-US>3.1.1.</span>项目功能介绍图</span></b><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc14607"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>3.2</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc14607'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>交互设计</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>3.2.1.</span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>设计原则及设计亮点<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>设计原则<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小程序以白绿为主色，体现绿色环保的主题，搭配不同亮度，色调的绿色，使整体界面设计统一，四种<span
class=GramE>绿分别</span>为四类垃圾分类主打色。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>设计亮点<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>①使用卡通人物作为小程序主人公，以典<span
class=GramE>典</span>为名，并用其作为漫画主人公使小程序更有趣吸引人，便于用户记忆，符合小程序的“趣”。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>②剧情测试板块使用统一<span
lang=EN-US>logo</span>，使整个板块有统一感。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>③以卡片的形式展示识别结果、科普知识、每日环保便于浏览。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>3.2.2</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>页面展示及使用说明<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:24.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:24.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc31158"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>3.3</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc31158'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>未来展望</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>①以“垃圾分类<span class=GramE>趣</span>宝典”公众号为宣传手段，推出垃圾分类相关文章和相关服务，吸引更多用户使用小程序。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>②丰富剧情测试板块场景及场景内容，增设更多类型场景，进一步科普垃圾分类小知识，让用户在故事体验中记忆垃圾所属类别，提高用户垃圾分类能力。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>③按期推出垃圾分类相关漫画介绍垃圾分类知识，提高用户分类意识。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:28.0pt'><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>④收集用户体验反馈，不断改进小程序。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US><span

</span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:仿宋'>数据端</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:仿宋'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:仿宋'>图<span lang=EN-US>4.1.1.</span>系统总体框架设计图</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>补充：<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>①客户端中包括两个部分：<span
class=GramE>微信小</span>程序和后台管理系统。<span class=GramE>微信小</span>程序用的原生，后台管理员系统用的<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>html+css+js</span></span>。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>②服务端基于<span
lang=EN-US>php</span>语言，以<span lang=EN-US>MVC</span>的软件设计模式开发。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>③数据端中使用的是<span
lang=EN-US>MySQL</span>关系型数据库管理系统。</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc27931"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>4.2</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc27931'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>项目引用技术情况</span></b></span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:仿宋;color:white;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>表</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:仿宋'>4.2.1.</span><span
style='font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:仿宋'>项目引用技术情况表</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc27634"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>4.3</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc27634'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>项目技术亮点</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>①页面<span
lang=EN-US>UI</span>设计有趣，用户体验良好。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>②搜索垃圾形式多样。可满足不同类型用户需求，用户覆盖面积大。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>③具体分类显示：数据库中垃圾数据多，后端处理数据困难，前端调用数据需优化代码，使垃圾以字母排序显示，并且界面显示速度快。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>④字母跳转：点击字母，跳转到第一个对应首字母的垃圾。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>⑤每日一句：随机调用服务器上的图片。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:left;
text-indent:-36.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:1;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1'><a
name="_Toc14040"><![if !supportLists]><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:黑体'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>五、<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><![endif]><b><span
style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>小程序体验码</span></b></a><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=center style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=center style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=center style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:
center;text-indent:0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=center style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:
center;text-indent:0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:left;
text-indent:-36.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:1;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1'><a
name="_Toc17400"><![if !supportLists]><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:黑体'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>六、<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><![endif]><b><span
style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>团队介绍及分工</span></b></a><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:15.0pt;font-family:黑体;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc5292"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>6.1</span></b></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc5292'><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>团队介绍</span></b></span><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>起初，本项目成员怀着对社会做点有意义的事的小小念头，在了解到如今垃圾分类的风头渐渐减小，人们对国家垃圾分类相关政策的不满，搭乘上了垃圾分类的末班车，拉上了典<span
class=GramE>典</span>（小程序中的指南精灵），倾情推出了这款小程序。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:28.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>希望能让看到渺小我们的有缘人，对国家的垃圾分类政策多一点支持。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='text-align:left;text-indent:0cm;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc7160"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:【何尼玛】扭曲体'>6.2</span></b></a><span
